sites, it is not strictly necessary to check all of\\n179: // these relationships (for example, for forward convolution, we compute\\n180: // the size of output ourselves, so we don't actually need to check\\n181: // output.  However, writing a single function that does everything\\n182: // means we get to reuse it for both forwards and all backwards\\n183: // variants, even when the set of \\\"real\\\" inputs varies.  The magic of\\n184: // relational computing!\\n185: //\\n186: // (There is one downside, which is that it is slightly harder to write\\n187: // error messages which are able to distinguish between real inputs\\n188: // (which the user can change) and computed inputs (which the user can\\n189: // only indirectly affect).  It would be an interesting exercise to\\n190: // come up with a general framework to handle such situations.)\\n191: inline void convolution_shape_check(\\n192:     CheckedFrom c,\\n193:     const weight_size.size())\\n223:   bool has_dilation = !dilation.empty();\\n224:   auto dim = input_size.size();\\n225:   std::vector<T> output_size(dim);\\n226:   output_size[0] = However, writing a single function that does everything\n182: // means we get to reuse it for both forwards and all backwards\n183: // variants, even when the set of \"real\" inputs varies. \\n199: template<typename scalar_t, typename param_t, template<typename T> class VarTransform>\\n200: static std::tuple<Tensor,Tensor> batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template(\\n201:     const Tensor& input, const Tensor& running_mean, const Tensor& running_var,\\n202:     double momentum, double eps, Tensor& save_mean, Tensor& save_var_transform) {\\n203: \\n204:   using accscalar_t = \\n223:   auto running_mean_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(running_mean);\\n224:   auto running_var_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(running_var);\\n225: \\n226:   if (all_contiguous) {\\n227:     auto _mean = at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\\n228:     auto _var_sum = at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\\n229:     auto _mean_a = _mean.accessor<opmath_t, 1>();\\n230:     auto _var_sum_a = _var_sum.accessor<opmath_t, 1>();\\n231:     auto momentum_ = static_cast<opmath_t>(momentum);\\n232: \\n233: .declare_static_shape(input.sizes(), /*squash_dims=*/1)\\n260:       .check_all_same_dtype(false)\\n261:       .promote_inputs_to_common_dtype(false)\\n262:       .build();\\n263: \\n264: \\n289: template<typename scalar_t, typename param_t, template<typename T> class VarTransform>\\n290: static std::tuple<Tensor,Tensor> batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template(\\n291:     const Tensor&
